namespace = giga_edicts

#Search for moons
country_event = {
	id = giga_edicts.1
	title = "giga_edicts.1.name"
	desc = "giga_edicts.1.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_cold_barren
	show_sound = event_sensor_ping
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { name = "giga_edicts.1.a" }

	immediate = {
		every_planet_within_border = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					giga_is_barren_cn = yes
					giga_is_frozen = yes 
					giga_is_molten = yes
				}
				planet_size >= 5
				planet_size <= 7
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = attack_moon_candidate
					has_planet_flag = crisis_vital_planet
				}
			}
			add_modifier = { modifier = "attack_moon_candidate" days = -1 }
		}
	}
}

#Search for planets
country_event = {
	id = giga_edicts.2
	title = "giga_edicts.2.name"
	desc = "giga_edicts.2.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_cold_barren
	show_sound = event_sensor_ping
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { name = "giga_edicts.2.a" }

	immediate = {
		every_planet_within_border = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					giga_is_barren_cn = yes
					giga_is_toxic = yes
					giga_is_frozen = yes 
					giga_is_molten = yes
				}
				planet_size >= 25
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = attack_planet_candidate
					has_planet_flag = crisis_vital_planet
				}
			}
			add_modifier = { modifier = "attack_planet_candidate" days = -1 }
		}
	}
}

# asteroid industry candidates
country_event = {
	id = giga_edicts.3
	title = "giga_edicts.3.name"
	desc = "giga_edicts.3.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_mining_station
	show_sound = event_sensor_ping
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { name = "giga_edicts.3.a" }

	immediate = {
		every_planet_within_border = {
			limit = {
				has_planet_flag = @asteroid_industry_candidate_flag
				nor = {
					has_planet_flag = has_megastructure
					has_planet_flag = megastructure
				}
			}
			add_modifier = { modifier = giga_asteroid_industry_candidate_marked }
		}
	}
}

# Map the stars
country_event = {
	id = giga_edicts.4
	title = "giga_edicts.4.name"
	desc = "giga_edicts.4.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_star_chart
	show_sound = event_sensor_ping
	is_triggered_only = yes



	###########################################
	### Class O ###############################
	###########################################
	option = {
		name = "giga_edicts.4.o.on"
		trigger = { has_event_chain = giga_class_o NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_o_stars_disabled } }
		hidden_effect = {
			end_event_chain = giga_class_o
			country_event = { id = giga_edicts.4 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "giga_edicts.4.o.off"
		trigger = { NOT = { has_event_chain = giga_class_o } NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_o_stars_disabled } }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = giga_edicts.4 }
			begin_event_chain = {
				event_chain = giga_class_o
				target = root
			}
			every_system = {
				limit = { is_star_class = sc_giga_o_star }
				save_event_target_as = giga_mapped_system
				root = {
					if = {		limit = { NOT = { has_point_of_interest = { poi = giga_class_o_001 } } } create_point_of_interest = { id = giga_class_o_001 name = "giga_mapped_star" desc = "giga_mapped_star_desc" event_chain = giga_class_o location = prev } }
					else_if = {	limit = { NOT = { has_point_of_interest = { poi = giga_class_o_002 } } } create_point_of_interest = { id = giga_class_o_002 name = "giga_mapped_star" desc = "giga_mapped_star_desc" event_chain = giga_class_o location = prev } }
					else_if = {	limit = { NOT = { has_point_of_interest = { poi = giga_class_o_003 } } } create_point_of_interest = { id = giga_class_o_003 name = "giga_mapped_star" desc = "giga_mapped_star_desc" event_chain = giga_class_o location = prev } }
					else_if = {	limit = { NOT = { has_point_of_interest = { poi = giga_class_o_004 } } } create_point_of_interest = { id = giga_class_o_004 name = "giga_mapped_star" desc = "giga_mapped_star_desc" event_chain = giga_class_o location = prev } }
					else_if = {	limit = { NOT = { has_point_of_interest = { poi = giga_class_o_005 } } } create_point_of_interest = { id = giga_class_o_005 name = "giga_mapped_star" desc = "giga_mapped_star_desc" event_chain = giga_class_o location = prev } }
					else_if = {	limit = { NOT = { has_point_of_interest = { poi = giga_class_o_006 } } } create_point_of_interest = { id = giga_class_o_006 name = "giga_mapped_star" desc = "giga_mapped_star_desc" event_chain = giga_class_o location = prev } }
					else_if = {	limit = { NOT = { has_point_of_interest = { poi = giga_class_o_007 } } } create_point_of_interest = { id = giga_class_o_007 name = "giga_mapped_star" desc = "giga_mapped_star_desc" event_chain = giga_class_o location = prev } }
					else_if = {	limit = { NOT = { has_point_of_interest = { poi = giga_class_o_008 } } } create_point_of_interest = { id = giga_class_o_008 name = "giga_mapped_star" desc = "giga_mapped_star_desc" event_chain = giga_class_o location = prev } }

		name = "giga_edicts.4.c.on"
		trigger = { has_event_chain = giga_class_f }
		hidden_effect = {
			end_event_chain = giga_class_f
			country_event = { id = giga_edicts.4 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "giga_edicts.4.g.on"
		trigger = { has_event_chain = giga_class_m }
		hidden_effect = {
			end_event_chain = giga_class_m
			country_event = { id = giga_edicts.4 }
		}
	}

	option = {

	### Pulsar ################################
	###########################################
	option = {
		name = "giga_edicts.4.i.on"
		trigger = { has_event_chain = giga_pulsar }
		hidden_effect = {
			end_event_chain = giga_pulsar
			country_event = { id = giga_edicts.4 }
		}
	}

	option = {
